#000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eAuthentication \u0026amp; Role Separation\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003ePrevents unauthorized relay access and privilege misuse\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eEnsure each user has their own account with only the permissions they need (e.g., Operator, Engineer). Remove default or unused credentials.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp style\u003d\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eSecure Firmware \u0026amp; Configuration Updates\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003ePrevents unauthorized or malicious software uploads\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eOnly allow firmware/configuration updates using verified, signed images through secure tools or physical access. Keep update logs.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp style\u003d\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e3\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eNetwork \u0026amp; Protocol Hardening\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003ePrevents spoofed messages, unauthorized remote access, VLAN abuse\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eDisable unused services like HTTP, Telnet, or FTP. Use authenticated communication for SCADA protocols (IEC 61850, DNP3). Whitelist IPs.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp style\u003d\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e4\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eTime Synchronization \u0026amp; Logging Protection\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eEnsures forensic accuracy and prevents log tampering or replay attacks\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eUse authenticated SNTP or IRIG-B for time. Protect event logs (SER, fault records) from unauthorized deletion or overwrite.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp style\u003d\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e5\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eCustom Logic Integrity Protection\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003ePrevents logic-based sabotage or backdoors in protection schemes\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eMonitor and restrict changes to programmable logic (trip equations, control rules). Maintain version history and hash verification.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp style\u003d\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e6\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003ePhysical Interface Hardening\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eBlocks unauthorized access via debug ports or jumpers\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd style\u003d\"vertical-align:middle;border:1px solid #000000;padding:16px\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eDisable, seal, or password-protect physical interfaces like USB, serial, or Ethernet service ports.
